msg:My friends and I stayed at the Crowne Plaza for one night while transitioning to Guilin. 

The hotel was in a good location next to the beach, and we were happy to have good rooms overlooking the sea view. 

For dinner, I went to the Chinese restaurant at the hotel, and they had excellent service and food (the beef fried rice is a must to have). 

The breakfast in the morning was great, with a wide range of options available. 

It would have been nice for the lounge to extend its opening times as they close quite early, and we could not access it. 

Overall, we had a good stay and would recommend this hotel to anyone visiting Beihai.

msg:When traveling in Beihai, stay at Crown. I worked overtime all night on Friday night, and left the company to go to Pudong Airport early on Saturday morning. I had long thought about giving myself a good vacation after working overtime all night. My goal is very clear, to drive away fatigue, release stress, relax, and be happy. I originally planned to stay on the beach on Weizhou Island for 4 days when I arrived in Beihai, but the various reviews of the island on the Internet discouraged me, so I might as well find a hotel to take a good look at the sea view. I bought a package from a certain airline, 4 days and 3 nights with airport pick-up and two breakfasts, and an additional 200 consumption coupons. I made an appoin**ent with the hotel for flight pick-up in advance. It took less than 15 minutes from exiting the cabin door to getting on the hotel pick-up car, which was very smooth. After arriving at the hotel, the front desk guy received me very warmly. When he learned that I came to the hotel alone to relax, he was very considerate to upgrade me to a high-floor sea view room. The very good front sea view greatly restored my body and mind. On the day of check-in, I happened to meet the Guangxi Alumni Association of my alma mater. I took a photo and said hello to alumni I didn‚Äôt know, haha. The guest room knew that I was staying in the hotel, so they gave me enough water and tea bags. The hotel breakfast is quite rich, the only shortcoming is that the pastry chef is not good, which needs to be improved. It is no problem to eat full, and the variety is rich enough. Fruits are delivered every day, and dinner can be taken out or solved in the hotel. Anyway, the package includes consumption coupons, so I can't waste them. After four days, I feel happy and full of energy. Now I advise everyone to stay in this Crown Hotel when they drive to Beihai! !

The room is very spacious and fully equipped. The disadvantage of the room is that there is no balcony in the hardware design. Breakfast is also very rich. I would like to make two comments about the service. It is not a big problem but it can be done better: 1) There are fried buns for breakfast. I asked the waiter (who was dressed as a kitchen staff, not the person responsible for clearing the table) what the fillings of the buns were. It's barbecued pork, and the pan-fried buns are stuffed with barbecued pork. I haven't eaten them before, so I checked them carefully. After I took them, I found out they were stuffed with pickles. I took a few more and found they were still stuffed with pickles, so I asked the waiter. It may be a bit much to know what the filling is, but the restaurant should at least put a small sign on the side to explain the ingredients of the filling. This should be what a five-star hotel should do. 2) The outdoor swimming pool will close the umbrellas on Saturday 12/9 After leaving, I asked the on-site staff and they said that the outdoor swimming pool was planned to be closed on 12/10. My opinion is that if it is closed on 12/10 (not to mention that the maximum temperature on 12/10 is 28¬∞C and sunny), then the umbrellas should be closed on 12/10. After all, the outdoor swimming pool will still be open on 12/9. In addition, I did not see on Ctrip that hotel outdoor swimming pools are closed seasonally. When I came to Beihai, choosing a hotel with an outdoor swimming pool was an important consideration. The hotel lacked information disclosure. Therefore, I only give 3 points for hotel service.

1. The five-star hotel closest to Yintan, with a great view of the sea view; 20 minutes' drive from the railway station, the distance is moderate.
2. The buffet restaurant on the first floor and the Chinese restaurant on the second floor are at the level of a five-star hotel.
3. The overall service attitude is good, kind and courteous.
4. At the time of check-in, the front desk in the lobby was unable to meet my two consecutive orders without changing rooms, so I offered two drink coupons to apologize, although the hotel did not need to do so.
4. There is a children‚Äôs pool, a children‚Äôs inflatable castle, a children‚Äôs playroom, and a bubble bath for children in the afternoon. Children will not be bored.

insufficient:
1. The room delivery service. The card was written in 20 minutes. As a result, I made three calls. After repeated confirmations by the room service, I told me that it would arrive in 45 minutes to an hour. The time I called is 5:30 in the afternoon, which is not the peak meal time, why is it so long? If you can‚Äôt do it three times, it‚Äôs recommended not to write for 20 minutes, otherwise it‚Äôs a false propaganda: when I called for the third time and wanted to order a meal, I actually said that the spaghetti with meat sauce and Hainanese chicken rice were gone, so I could only order don‚Äôt of. In fact, these two items are relatively basic and should not be out of stock.
2. The bar on the 21st floor. I was eager to go up and see what cocktails there were. As a result, the wine list was only one or two thousand more red wine than the lobby bar. If there is no cocktail, do people only drink beer and red wine, and there are few choices and no white wine.
3. Speaking of white wine, there are a lot of seafood to choose from in the buffet restaurant on the first floor, but the wine is only red wine, not white wine. Eat seafood or white meat with white wine, and red meat with red wine. It is recommended to improve it.
4. The coffee in the restaurant on the first floor...really hard to say. It is recommended to change coffee beans as soon as possible. The business chain Youyi Hotel where I lived in Nanning before, the coffee is better than this.

Summary: I can feel that the basic facilities of the hotel and the service attitude of the staff are all five-star, including helping with luggage, children's chairs and children's tableware in the restaurant, and you can experience good intentions. However, the details, and the difference between a five-star beachfront resort hotel and a five-star business hotel in the city, have not yet been determined. I'm here for vacation, but the hotel doesn't give me the feeling of vacation. Many children's activities are also found by me taking the initiative to find or by luck. What projects and activities did you choose to make me feel at home and linger.
